)@@G@@    DEFINITION OF ACCOUNT NUMBER FORMAT   @[@@@@.     @G@@@@.         ACNZ
)@@G@@COUNT NUMBER FORMAT IS SPECIFIED BELOW BY SUCCESSIVE CALLS  @E@@@@.     OA
)@@G@@    ON THE PROC AFIELD.  THE FORM OF THE CALL IS:     @[@@@@.     @D@@@@OB
)@@G@@.                   AFIELD  LENGTH  SPEC1,...,SPECN   @[@@@@.     @G@@@@OC
)@@G@@.         EACH CALL SPECIFIES ONE FIELD IN THE ACCOUNT NUMBER.  ALL     OD
)@@G@@@G@@@@.         FIELDS IN THE ACCOUNT NUMBER EXCEPT THE LAST ONE MAKE UPOE
)@@G@@ THE  @G@@@@.         MANAGER PART OF THE ACCOUNT NUMBER.  THE LAST FIELOF
)@@G@@D IS THE    @G@@@@.         USER PART.  LENGTH IS THE NUMBER OF CHARACTEOG
)@@G@@RS IN A FIELD.    @G@@@@.         SPEC1,...SPECN SPECIFY THE CHARACTERS OH
)@@G@@ALLOWED IN A FIELD.     @F@@@@.         SPECN MAY SPECIFY A LETTER('A',.OI
)@@G@@..,'Z'), ALL LETTERS    @F@@@@.         ('LETTERS'), A DIGIT('0',...,'9'OJ
)@@G@@), ALL DIGITS('DIGITS'),@F@@@@.         A DASH('-'), OR ALL OF THE PRECEOK
)@@G@@EDING CHARACTERS('ALL').@[@@@@.     @F@@@@.         AFIELD MUST BE CALLEOL
)@@G@@D AT LEAST TWICE.  THE SUM OF THE   @D@@@@.         LENGTHS OF THE FIELDOM
)@@G@@S MUST NOT EXCEED 12.   @[@@@@.     @G@@@@.         EXAMPLE 1.  TO REQUION
)@@G@@RE THAT THE MANAGER PART OF AN ACCOUNT    @G@@@@.         NUMBER CONSISTOO
)@@G@@S OF ONE OF THE LETTERS A, B, OR C, FOLLOWED BY @G@@@@.         5 DIGITSOP
)@@G@@, AND THAT THE USER PART CONSIST OF ANY 6 CHARACTERS, @B@@@@.         THOQ
)@@G@@E FOLLOWING CALLS ARE NEEDED: @[@@@@.     @B@@@@.                   AFIEOR
)@@G@@LD  1  'A','B','C'@B@@@@.                   AFIELD  5  'DIGITS'   @A@@@@OS
)@@G@@.                   AFIELD  6  'ALL'@[@@@@.     @G@@@@.         EXAMPLE OT
)@@G@@2.  TO REQUIRE THAT THE MANAGER PART IS 7  DIGITS AND @G@@@@.         THOU
)@@G@@AT THE USER PART IS ANY 5 CHARACTERS, THE FOLLOWING CALLS   @^@@@@.     OV
)@@G@@    ARE NEEDED:   @[@@@@.     @B@@@@.                   AFIELD  7  'DIGIOW
)@@G@@TS'   @A@@@@.                   AFIELD  5  'ALL'@[@@@@.     @E@@@@.     OX
)@@G@@    DEFINE THE ACCOUNT FILE FORMAT FOR YOUR SITE HERE:@[@@@@.     @E@@@@OY
)@@G@@          AFIELD    6 'DIGITS'        . UOM MANAGER PART    @D@@@@      OZ
)@@G@@    AFIELD    6 'ALL'           . UOM USER PART @[@@@@.     @G@@@@.  .  PA
)@@G@@.  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  @[@@@@PB
)@@G@@.     @F@@@@.         THE FOLLOWING CODE PROCESSES SUBSCRIPTED LABELS PRPC
)@@G@@ODUCED@D@@@@.         BY PRECEEDING CALLS ON THE PROC AFIELD.     @[@@@@PD
)@@G@@.     @G@@@@          DO AFFLEN<2 ,M EQU 08       . ERROR IF LESS THAN 2PE
)@@G@@ FIELDS     @F@@@@SUM(1)    EQU       0                 . GET TOTAL OF FPF

)@@G@@C2,...,SPECN@[@@@@.     @F@@@@.         THIS PROC IS USED TO SPECIFY THETQ
)@@G@@ ACCOUNT NUMBER FORMAT  @G@@@@.         FOR AN INSTALLATION.  EACH CALL TR
)@@G@@ON AFIELD SPECIFIES A FIELD   @G@@@@.         LENGTH(LEN) AND THE CHARACTS
)@@G@@TERS THAT WILL BE ALLOWED IN THAT   @G@@@@.         FIELD(SPEC1,...,SPECTT
)@@G@@N).  ALL CALLS ON AFIELD EXCEPT THE LAST  @F@@@@.         CALL SPECIFY TTU
)@@G@@HE MANAGER PORTION OF THE ACCOUNT NUMBER. @G@@@@.         THE FINAL CALLTV
)@@G@@ ON AFIELD SPECIFIES THE USER PORTION OF THE    @G@@@@.         ACCOUNT TW
)@@G@@NUMBER.  AFIELD MUST BE CALLED AT LEAST TWICE.  THE   @G@@@@.         SUTX
)@@G@@M OF THE FIELD LENGTHS SPECIFIED ON ALL CALLS MUST BE LESS  @^@@@@.     TY
)@@G@@    THAN TWELVE.  @[@@@@.     @F@@@@.         SPECN MAY SPECIFY A LETTERTZ
)@@G@@('A',...'Z'), ALL LETTERS     @F@@@@.         ('LETTERS'), A DIGIT('0',.UA
)@@G@@..,'9'), ALL DIGITS('DIGITS'),@F@@@@.         A DASH('-'), OR ALL OF THEUB
)@@G@@ PRECEEDING CHARACTERS('ALL').@[@@@@.     @G@@@@.  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  UC
)@@G@@.  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  @B@@@@P         PROC    UD
)@@G@@  *2                .   @B@@@@AFIELD*   NAME                        .   UE
)@@G@@@F@@@@          ON        AFMLEN=0          . PROCESS ON FIRST PASS ONLYUF
)@@G@@@[@@@@.     @C@@@@LETTERS   EQU       +007777777760000000000000D .@C@@@@UG
)@@G@@DIGITS    EQU       +000000000000000077740000D .@C@@@@ALL       EQU     UH
)@@G@@  +007777777764000077740000D .@[@@@@.     @E@@@@N         EQU       AFFLUI
)@@G@@EN+1          . ADVANCE COUNTER     @G@@@@          DO P<3 ,M EQU 080   UJ
)@@G@@        . ERROR IF LESS THAN 2 FIELDS     @F@@@@          DO P(1,1)<1 ,MUK
)@@G@@ EQU 081      . ERROR IF FIELD LENGTH < 1 @E@@@@AFFLEN**(N) EQU     P(1,UL
)@@G@@1)            . RECORD FIELD LENGTH @[@@@@.     @B@@@@Q*        PROC    UM
)@@G@@  *0                .   @B@@@@R(1)      EQU       +0D               .   UN
)@@G@@@B@@@@S         EQU       P(2,I)            .   @C@@@@          DO S='LEUO

)@@G@@GITS   .    @B@@@@          DO S='ALL' ,R(1) EQU ALL    .   @B@@@@      UQ
)@@G@@    DO S<64 ,R(1) EQU +1D*/(71-S) . @B@@@@R(1)      EQU       R(1)**ALL UR
)@@G@@        .   @F@@@@          DO R(1)=0 ,M EQU 082        . ERROR IF BAD SUS

)@@G@@    END                         .   @[@@@@.     @B@@@@I         DO P(2) UU

)@@G@@.         AFATYP AREG,ADDR,X AFRSAU,JUMPAU AFRSAM,JUMPAM AFRSIM,JUMPIM  UY
)@@G@@@[@@@@.     @F@@@@.         THIS PROC DETERMINES THE TYPE OF AN ACCOUNT UZ
)@@G@@NUMBER.     @[@@@@.     @G@@@@.         AREG DEFINES THE FIRST OF TWO A VA
)@@G@@REGISTERS THAT WILL BE USED   @G@@@@.         TO HOLD AN ACCOUNT NUMBER.VB
)@@G@@  ADDR,X (X IS AN INDEX REGISTER    @F@@@@.         MODIFYING ADDR) IS TVC
)@@G@@HE ADDRESS OF THE ACCOUNT NUMBER.   @F@@@@.         ADDR MUST NOT POINT VD
)@@G@@TO THE A-REGISTER SPECIFIED BY AREG.@[@@@@.     @G@@@@.         A JUMP IVE
)@@G@@S GENERATED TO JUMPAU, JUMPAM, OR JUMPIM DEPENDING    @G@@@@.         UPVF
)@@G@@ON WHETHER THE ACCOUNT NUMBER IS FOR AN ACCOUNT USER, AN    @G@@@@.     VG
)@@G@@    ACCOUNT MANAGER, OR THE INSTALLATION MANAGER.  THE LAST THREE @G@@@@VH
)@@G@@.         FIELDS ARE OPTIONAL AND MAY OCCUR IN ANY ORDER. IF ONE OF     VI
)@@G@@@F@@@@.         THE LAST THREE FIELDS IS OMITTED, CONTROL PASSES TO     VJ
)@@G@@@F@@@@.         THE NEXT INSTRUCTION FOLLOWING THE PROC CALL FOR THE    VK
)@@G@@@G@@@@.         TYPE OF ACCOUNT NUMBER CORRESPONDING TO THE MISSING FIELVL
)@@G@@D.    @E@@@@.         IF AFATYP IS USED IN NON-EXEC CODE, THE JUMP TO   VM
)@@G@@@B@@@@.         JUMPIM WILL NEVER BE TAKEN.     @[@@@@.     @F@@@@.     VN
)@@G@@    AFTER THE PROC IS EXECUTED, IF THE ACCOUNT NUMBER WAS   @G@@@@.     VO
)@@G@@    FOR AN ACCOUNT USER,  THE REGISTERS SPECIFIED BY AREG WILL    @F@@@@VP
)@@G@@.         CONTAIN THE ACCOUNT NUMBER OF THE USERS ACCOUNT MANAGER.@E@@@@VQ
)@@G@@.         OTHERWIST, THE REGISTERS WILL CONTAIN THE ORIGINAL@ @@@@.     VR
)@@G@@    ACCOUNT NUMBER.     @[@@@@.     @G@@@@.  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  VS
)@@G@@.  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  @B@@@@P         PROC          VT
)@@G@@              .   @B@@@@AFATYP*   NAME                        .   @[@@@@VU
)@@G@@.     @D@@@@.         DETERMINE WHICH EXITS HAVE BEEN SPECIFIED   @[@@@@VV
)@@G@@.     @B@@@@Q*        PROC                        .   @B@@@@J         EQVW
)@@G@@U       I+1               .   @C@@@@          DO P(J,1)=AFRSAU ,JAU*(1) VX
)@@G@@EQU J .     @C@@@@          DO P(J,1)=AFRSAM ,JAM*(1) EQU J .     @C@@@@VY
)@@G@@          DO P(J,1)=AFRSIM ,JIM*(1) EQU J .     @B@@@@          END     VZ
)@@G@@                    .   @[@@@@.     @D@@@@I         DO P-2 , Q . DETERMIWA
)@@G@@NE JUMP DESTINATIONS    @[@@@@.     @B@@@@AR        EQU       P(1,1)    WB
)@@G@@        .   @D@@@@ANUM      EQUF      P(1,2),P(1,3)     . ACCOUNT NUMBERWC
)@@G@@@[@@@@.     @ @@@@.         LOAD ACCOUNT NUMBER @[@@@@.     @E@@@@      WD
)@@G@@    DL        AR,ANUM           . LOAD ACCOUNT NUMBER @D@@@@          ONWE
)@@G@@        AFEXEC**((JIM(1)>0)++(JAM(1)>0)) .@F@@@@          DTE       AR,AWF
)@@G@@FIMGR         . INSTALLATION MANAGER?     @B@@@@          J         AROUWG
)@@G@@ND            .   @D@@@@          J         JUMPIM            . YES,JUMPWH
)@@G@@IM NO @B@@@@AROUND                                .   @D@@@@          OFWI
)@@G@@F       AFEXEC**((JIM(1)>0)++(JAM(1)>0)) .@[@@@@.     @B@@@@.         COWJ
)@@G@@NSTRUCT ACCOUNT MANAGER NUMBER@[@@@@.     @C@@@@          ON        (AFMWK
)@@G@@LEN<6)++(6<AFMLEN) .    @E@@@@          DSL       AR,6*(12-AFMLEN)  . SHWL
)@@G@@IFT OFF USER PART @E@@@@          LDSL      AR,6*(12-AFMLEN)  . SHIFT ZEWM
)@@G@@RO'S BACK ON@C@@@@          OFF       (AFMLEN<6)++(6<AFMLEN) .    @B@@@@WN
)@@G@@          DO AFMLEN<3 , ;             .   @D@@@@          A         AR,(WO
)@@G@@+'      '*/(-AFMLEN*6)) .     @B@@@@          DO (2<AFMLEN)**(AFMLEN<6) WP
)@@G@@, ; . @C@@@@          A,U       AR,'      '*/(-AFMLEN*6) .  @B@@@@      WQ
)@@G@@    DO AFMLEN<7 , ;             .   @B@@@@          L         AR+1,SPACEWR
)@@G@@S       .   @B@@@@          DO (6<AFMLEN)**(AFMLEN<9) , ; . @D@@@@      WS
)@@G@@    A         AR+1,('      '*/((6-AFMLEN)*6)) . @B@@@@          DO 8<AFMWT
)@@G@@LEN , ;             .   @D@@@@          A,U       AR+1,'      '*/((6-AFMWU
)@@G@@LEN)*6) .   @[@@@@.     @D@@@@.         TEST FOR ACCOUNT MANAGER OR ACCOWV
)@@G@@UNT USER    @[@@@@.     @C@@@@          ON        (JAU(1)>0)++(JAM(1)>0)WW
)@@G@@ .    @B@@@@          DO JAM(1)>0 , ;             .   @G@@@@          TNWX
)@@G@@E       AR+(5<AFMLEN),ANUM+(5<AFMLEN) . ACCOUNT MANAGER?    @B@@@@      WY
)@@G@@    DO JAM(1)=0 , ;             .   @G@@@@          TE        AR+(5<AFMLWZ
)@@G@@EN),ANUM+(5<AFMLEN) . ACCOUNT MANAGER?    @D@@@@          DO JAM(1)>0 , XA
)@@G@@J JUMPAM      . YES, JUMPAM   @D@@@@          DO JAU(1)>0 , J JUMPAU    XB
)@@G@@  . NO,JUMPAU     @C@@@@          OFF       (JAU(1)>0)++(JAM(1)>0) .    XC
)@@G@@@]@@@@GOODBY    . @[@@@@.     @C@@@@          DO JAU(1)>0 ,JUMPAU EQU P(XD
)@@G@@JAU(1),2) . @C@@@@          DO JAM(1)>0 ,JUMPAM EQU P(JAM(1),2) . @C@@@@XE
)@@G@@          DO JIM(1)>0 ,JUMPIM EQU P(JIM(1),2) . @[@@@@.     @B@@@@      XF
)@@G@@    DO JAU(1)=0 ,JUMPAU EQU GOODBY .@B@@@@          DO JAM(1)=0 ,JUMPAM XG
)@@G@@EQU GOODBY .@B@@@@          DO JIM(1)=0 ,JUMPIM EQU GOODBY .@[@@@@.     XH
)@@G@@@B@@@@          END                         .   @G@@@@/  .  .  .  .  .  XI
)@@G@@.  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  @[@@@@.     @D@@@@XJ
)@@G@@.         AFBILD    MREGS,MPART,XM  UREGS,UPART,XU    @[@@@@.     @G@@@@XK
)@@G@@.         THIS PROC BUILDS AN ACCOUNT NUMBER OUT OF A MANAGER PART AND  XL
)@@G@@@^@@@@.         A USER PART.  @[@@@@.     @G@@@@.         MREGS SPECIFIEXM
)@@G@@S THE FIRST OF A PAIR OF A-REGISTERS TO BE USED.@G@@@@.         LIKEWISEXN
)@@G@@ UREGS.  THE PAIRS OF REGISTERS SPECIFIED BY MREGS    @F@@@@.         ANXO
)@@G@@D UREGS MUST NOT OVERLAP.  THE COMPLETE ACCOUNT NUMBER@E@@@@.         WIXP
)@@G@@LL BE BUILT IN MREGS.  UREGS WILL BE DESTROYED. @[@@@@.     @F@@@@.     XQ
)@@G@@    MPART IS THE LOCTION OF A DOUBLE WORD WHOSE FIRST AFMLEN@G@@@@.     XR
)@@G@@    CHARACTERS CONTAIN THE MANAGER PART OF AN ACCOUNT NUMBER.     @E@@@@XS
)@@G@@.         XM IS AN INDEX REGISTER WHICH MODIFIES MPART.     @G@@@@.     XT
)@@G@@    IF MPART IS NOT SPECIFIED, THEN MREGS MUST CONTAIN THE MANAGER@#@@@@XU
)@@G@@.         PART.   @[@@@@.     @F@@@@.         UPART IS THE LOCTION OF A XV
)@@G@@DOUBLE WORD WHOSE FIRST AFULEN@F@@@@.         CHARACTERS CONTAIN THE USEXW
)@@G@@R PART OF AN ACCOUNT NUMBER.  @E@@@@.         XU IS AN INDEX REGISTER WHXX
)@@G@@ICH MODIFIES UPART.     @G@@@@.         IF UPART IS NOT SPECIFIED, THEN XY
)@@G@@UREGS MUST CONTAIN THE USER   @#@@@@.         PART.   @[@@@@.     @G@@@@XZ
)@@G@@.  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  YA
)@@G@@@B@@@@P         PROC                        .   @B@@@@AFBILD*   NAME    YB
)@@G@@                    .   @D@@@@MPART     EQUF      P(1,2),P(1,3)     . MAYC
)@@G@@NAGER PART  @D@@@@UPART     EQUF      P(2,2),P(2,3)     . USER PART     YD
)@@G@@@G@@@@AFBLEN    EQU       12-AFMLEN-AFULEN  . # BLANKS AFTER ACCOUNT NUMYE
)@@G@@BER   @F@@@@EASY      EQU       (AFMLEN=6)**(AFULEN=6) . EASY MEANS LESSYF
)@@G@@ CODE @F@@@@          DO P<3 , +08                . ERROR IF TOO FEW FIEYG
)@@G@@LDS   @B@@@@DIFF      EQU       P(1,1)-P(2,1)     .   @G@@@@          DOYH
)@@G@@ (-2<DIFF)**(DIFF<2) , +09 . ERROR IF A-REG PAIRS OVERLAP   @B@@@@      YI
)@@G@@                                .   @B@@@@          ON        EASY      YJ
)@@G@@        .   @E@@@@          DO P(1)>1 , LA P(1,1),MPART . LOAD MANAGER PYK
)@@G@@ART   @D@@@@          DO P(1)>1 , ;               . COMBINE PARTS @B@@@@YL
)@@G@@          LA        P(1,1)+1,UPART    .   @B@@@@          DO P(1)=1 , ; YM
)@@G@@              .   @B@@@@          LA        P(1,1)+1,P(2,1)   .   @B@@@@YN
)@@G@@          OFF       EASY              .   @B@@@@                        YO
)@@G@@              .   @B@@@@          ON        EASY=0            .   @B@@@@YP
)@@G@@          DO (P(1)>1)**(AFMLEN<7) , ; .   @E@@@@          LA        P(1,YQ
)@@G@@1),MPART      . LOAD MANAGER PART   @B@@@@          DO (P(1)>1)**(AFMLENYR
)@@G@@>6) , ; .   @B@@@@          DL        P(1,1),MPART      .   @B@@@@      YS
)@@G@@    DO (P(2)>1)**(AFULEN<7) , ; .   @D@@@@          LA        P(2,1),UPAYT
)@@G@@RT      . LOAD USER PART@B@@@@          DO (P(2)>1)**(AFULEN>6) , ; .   YU
)@@G@@@B@@@@          DL        P(2,1),UPART      .   @G@@@@          DSL     YV
)@@G@@  P(1,1),72-6*AFMLEN . SHIFT TRASH OFF MANAGER PART   @F@@@@          LDYW
)@@G@@SL      P(1,1),72-6*AFMLEN . SHIFT MANAGER PART BACK  @F@@@@          DSYX
)@@G@@L       P(2,1),72-6*AFULEN . SHIFT TRASH OFF USER PART@F@@@@          DOYY
)@@G@@ AFBLEN>0 , LDSL P(2,1),6*AFBLEN . POSITION USER PART @G@@@@            YZ
)@@G@@                          . COMBINE MANAGER AND USER PARTS  @B@@@@      ZA
)@@G@@    DO (AFMLEN<6)**(AFBLEN>5) , ; . @D@@@@          AA        P(1,1),P(2ZB
)@@G@@,1)     . (THIS WAY)    @B@@@@          DO (AFMLEN<6)**(AFBLEN<6) , ; . ZC
)@@G@@@D@@@@          DA        P(1,1),P(2,1)     . (OR THIS WAY) @B@@@@      ZD
)@@G@@    DO AFMLEN>5 , ;             .   @D@@@@          AA        P(1,1)+1,PZE
)@@G@@(2,1)+1 . (OR THIS WAY) @F@@@@                                      . ADZF
)@@G@@D ON TRAILING BLANKS    @B@@@@          DO 6<AFBLEN , ;             .   ZG
)@@G@@@G@@@@          DA        P(1,1),('            '*/(-6*(AFMLEN*AFULEN))) ZH
)@@G@@.     @B@@@@          DO (0<AFBLEN)**(AFBLEN<7) , ; . @F@@@@          AAZI
)@@G@@        P(1,1)+1,('      '*/(-6*(AFMLEN+AFULEN-6))) . @B@@@@          OFZJ
)@@G@@F       EASY=0            .   @B@@@@          END                       ZK
)@@G@@  .   @G@@@@/  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  ZL
)@@G@@.  .  .  .  @[@@@@.     @E@@@@.         PROC TO GENERATE CALLS TO ACCOUNZM
)@@G@@T FILE SUBROUTINES@[@@@@.     @G@@@@.         AFCALL  SUBROUTINE  ST(1),ZN
)@@G@@LOC(1) ST(2),LOC(2) ... ST(N),LOC(N)@F@@@@.      OR AFCALL  SUBROUTINE  ZO
)@@G@@ST(1),LOC(1) ST(2),LOC(2) ... LOC(N)@[@@@@.     @G@@@@.         THE SUBRZP
)@@G@@OUTINE IS CALLED AND THEN THE STATUS IS LOADED INTO   @G@@@@.         A4ZQ
)@@G@@.  IF THE STATUS EQUALS ST(N), THEN CONTROL IS PASSED TO    @G@@@@.     ZR
)@@G@@    LOC(N).  IF THE LAST FIELD CONTAINS ONLY ONE SUBFIELD, THEN IT@G@@@@ZS
)@@G@@.         IS A LOCATION TO WHICH CONTROL PASSES IF THE STATUS IS NOT    ZT
)@@G@@@B@@@@.         EQUAL TO ANY OF ST(1)...ST(N-1) @[@@@@.     @G@@@@.  .  ZU
)@@G@@.  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  @B@@@@ZV

)@@G@@ CHECK THE FORMAT OF AN ACCOUNT NUMBER    @B@@@@.         AND CLASSIFY AGT
)@@G@@CCOUNT NUMBER     @[@@@@.     @ @@@@.         USES:  A2,A3,A4     @[@@@@GU

)@@G@@        . $PH SAVE RETURN     @G@@@@          L,U       A2,AFFCHK       GY
)@@G@@  . $P SET SUBROUTINE TO AFFCHK     @B@@@@          S         A2,AFRSUB GZ
)@@G@@        .   @F@@@@AFBLEN    EQU       12-AFMLEN-AFULEN  . NUMBER OF BLANHA
)@@G@@KS IN UNUSED@G@@@@                                      .    PORTION OF HB
)@@G@@ACCOUNT NUMBER    @E@@@@AFBLMK    EQU       +1D*/(71-' ')     . MASK FORHC
)@@G@@ ONLY BLANK @[@@@@.     @F@@@@.         CODE TO CHANGE OLD FORMAT ACCOUNHD
)@@G@@T NUMBERS TO NEW FORMAT @F@@@@.         SHOULD BE INSERTED HERE.  ACCOUNHE
)@@G@@T NUMBER IS IN AFRANO.  @F@@@@.         IT SHOULD BE CONVERTED TO NEW FOHF
)@@G@@RMAT USING A2-A5 AND    @A@@@@.         THEN STORED IN AFRANO.    @[@@@@HG
)@@G@@.     @[@@@@.     @D@@@@          S         A0,AFRAN2         . $P SAVE HH
)@@G@@A0    @D@@@@          S         A1,X11            . $P SAVE A1    @F@@@@HI
)@@G@@          DL        A1,AFRANO         . $P GET ACCOUNT NUMBER     @F@@@@HJ
)@@G@@          L         A0,(1,0)          . $P SET FIELD COUNT TO 0   @F@@@@HK
)@@G@@AFF100    EX        AFF150,A0         . $T FINISHED ALL FIELDS?   @E@@@@HL
)@@G@@                                      . $A YES,AFF190 NO    @F@@@@      HM
)@@G@@                                . $P LOAD BIT MASK FOR FIELD@F@@@@      HN
)@@G@@    EX        AFF160,*A0        . $P LOAD COUNT FOR FIELD   @F@@@@      HO
)@@G@@                                . $P INCREMENT FIELD COUNT  @G@@@@AFF110HP

)@@G@@                                      . $ FIELD?@F@@@@          J       HR

)@@G@@  A2,077            .   @F@@@@AFF140    LDSC      A4,0,A3           . $PHU

)@@G@@                          .   @F@@@@          TE        A0,(1,AFFLEN)   IA

)@@G@@  . $A YES NO,AFF900    @F@@@@          TE,U      A3,' '            . $TIC
)@@G@@ IS CHARACTER A BLANK?  @E@@@@          J         AFF900            . $AID
)@@G@@ YES NO,AFF900    @F@@@@          DL        A4,(AFBLMK)       . $P LOAD IE

)@@G@@        .   @[@@@@/.    @[@@@@.     @#@@@@. TO ASSIGN A FILE@[@@@@.     IA
)@@G@@@B@@@@.         FIASG,'OPTS' PACKET,BITS NAME   @[@@@@.     @B@@@@P     IB
)@@G@@    PROC      *2                .   @B@@@@FIASG*    NAME                IC
)@@G@@        .   @[@@@@.     @B@@@@. FUNCTION TO GET BIT FOR 'BITS' LETTER.  ID
)@@G@@@[@@@@.     @B@@@@F         FUNC                        .   @B@@@@PBIT* IE
)@@G@@    NAME                        .   @D@@@@I DO 6 , DO M(0)*/(6-6*I)**077IF
)@@G@@=F(1) , END +F(2)  .    @D@@@@          END       +0                . STIG
)@@G@@RANGE BITS  @[@@@@.     @E@@@@M(0)      EQU       P(1,2)            . PIIH
)@@G@@CK UP MODE LETTERS@G@@@@B(0)      EQU       PBIT(013,001)+PBIT(032,002)+II
)@@G@@PBIT(035,004)+ ; F,U,X  @G@@@@                    PBIT(027,010)+PBIT(034IJ
)@@G@@,020)+PBIT(024,040)++; R,W,O  @C@@@@                    002*(P(2)>0)+040IK
)@@G@@*(P(0)>1) . @[@@@@.     @^@@@@. NOW GENERATE CODE     @[@@@@.     @D@@@@IL

)@@G@@B(0),P(1,1))  . ELSE L  @D@@@@          OFF       P(1)>0            . ANIO

)@@G@@          OFF       P(0)>1            . ANY OPTIONS ? @[@@@@.     @ @@@@IT

)@@G@@              .   @[@@@@.     @F@@@@. THIS PROCEDURE IS USED TO CALL THEIW

)@@G@@F     @F@@@@QR$FAW    FORM      12,6,18           . FORM FOR ACCESS WORDQU
)@@G@@S     @^@@@@P         PROC      *1  @#@@@@QUERIES*  NAME    @F@@@@QR$QC*QV
)@@G@@(0) EQU       0                 . INITIALIZE QUERY COUNTER  @F@@@@QR$LG*QW
)@@G@@(0) EQU       0                 . AND LINE GROUP COUNTER    @#@@@@      QX
)@@G@@    BRIEF   @E@@@@QR$GP*(0) EQU       GR$GP(0)+1        . COUNT GLOBAL PQY
)@@G@@ASSES @F@@@@QR$QLC*   EQU       &                 . SET LOC CTR FOR QUERQZ
)@@G@@IES   @E@@@@QR$TLC*   EQU       P(1,1)+(P(1)=0)*(QR$QLC+2) . AND TEXT   RA
)@@G@@@G@@@@ DO QR$GP(0)=2 , END                      . DON'T REDEFINE ON PASSRB
)@@G@@ 2    @C@@@@/. GROUP TO DEFINE TEXT TABLES FOR MESSAGES     @[@@@@.     RC
)@@G@@@^@@@@P         PROC      *1  @#@@@@MESSAGE** NAME    @G@@@@*         EQRD
)@@G@@U       $(QR$TLC)         . LABEL IS UNDER TEXT COUNTER     @F@@@@      RE
)@@G@@    QR$TXO    P(1,1)+(P(1)=0)     . OPEN TEXT ASSIMILATION  @#@@@@      RF
)@@G@@    END     @[@@@@.     @^@@@@P         PROC      *1  @F@@@@QR$TXO**  NARG
)@@G@@ME                        . OPEN TEXT ASSIMILATION    @]@@@@$(QR$TLC)   RH
)@@G@@@G@@@@N         EQU       1                 . SET COUNTER, THIS IS 1ST LRI
)@@G@@INE   @G@@@@QR$LG**(0) EQU      N                 . REMEMBER CURRENT LINRJ
)@@G@@E NUMBER    @G@@@@QR$LG**(N) EQU      $                 . REMEMBER STARTRK
)@@G@@ TEXT OF LINE N   @E@@@@QR$SK**(N) EQU      P(1,1)+(P(1,1)=0) . SET ITS RL
)@@G@@SKIP COUNT  @B@@@@          END       . FALL THRU TO 'TEXT' @[@@@@.     RM
)@@G@@@^@@@@P         PROC      *1  @G@@@@NEWLINE** NAME                      RN
)@@G@@  . BREAK- START BUILDING NEW LINE  @E@@@@N         EQU       QR$LG(0)  RO
)@@G@@        . GET LINE SERIAL NO  @E@@@@QR$LS*(N) EQU       $-QR$LG(N)      RP
)@@G@@  . COMPUTE ITS LENGTH  @G@@@@QR$LG*(N+1) EQU     $                 . RERQ
)@@G@@MEMBER WHERE NEW LINE STARTS  @E@@@@QR$SK*(N+1) EQU     P(1,1)+(P(1)=0) RR
)@@G@@  . SET ITS SKIP COUNT  @D@@@@QR$LG*(0) EQU       N+1               . CORS
)@@G@@UNT NEW LINE@#@@@@          END     @[@@@@.     @^@@@@P         PROC    RT
)@@G@@  *0  @#@@@@ENDMSG**  NAME    @#@@@@          QR$TXE  @#@@@@          ENRU
)@@G@@D     @[@@@@.     @^@@@@P         PROC      *0  @#@@@@QR$TXE**  NAME    RV
)@@G@@@G@@@@N         EQU       QR$LG(0)          . SERIAL NO OF PRECEDING LINRW
)@@G@@E     @F@@@@ DO N=0 , END                         . QUIT IF THERE WAS NORX
)@@G@@NE    @F@@@@QR$LS**(N) EQU      $-QR$LG(N)        . COMPUTE LAST LINE SIRY
)@@G@@ZE    @G@@@@ACWTBL                                . TABLE OF ACW'S FOR TRZ
)@@G@@HIS MESSAGE @G@@@@K DO N                                ; FOR ALL LINES SA
)@@G@@IN THIS GROUP     @F@@@@ , DO QR$LS(K)>0                      ; IF LINE SB
)@@G@@IS NOT VACUOUS    @D@@@@     , QR$FAW QR$SK(K),QR$LS(K),QR$LG(K) . GEN ASC
)@@G@@CW    @F@@@@TSA       EQU       QR$LG(1)          . ADDR OF 1ST TEXT WORSD
)@@G@@D     @F@@@@NAW       EQU       $-ACWTBL          . NUMBER OF ACCESS WORSE
)@@G@@DS    @F@@@@QR$NAW**(TSA) EQU   NAW               . REMEMBER HOW MANY LISF
)@@G@@NES   @F@@@@QR$AAW**(TSA) EQU   ACWTBL            . AND WHERE TABLE STARSG
)@@G@@TS    @#@@@@          END     @D@@@@/. USER LEVEL PROCS DEFINING QUERIESSH
)@@G@@ AND RESPONSES    @[@@@@.     @[@@@@.     @^@@@@P         PROC      *1  SI
)@@G@@@#@@@@QUERY**   NAME    @G@@@@*         EQU       $(QR$QLC)         . QUSJ
)@@G@@ERY LABEL UNDER QUERY CTR     @]@@@@$(QR$TLC)   @E@@@@TS                SK
)@@G@@                    . MARK TEXTABLE ORIGIN@G@@@@          QR$TXE        SL
)@@G@@              . CLOSE PREVIOUS TEXT, IF ANY     @G@@@@ DO TS=$ , 'FUDGE'SM
)@@G@@                    . FORCE TEXT LC BUMP FOR INDEXING @]@@@@$(QR$QLC)   SN
)@@G@@@F@@@@QN        EQU       QR$QC(0)+1        . QUERY NO FOR THIS QUERY   SO
)@@G@@@F@@@@RMT       EQU       P(0)=2            . ON IF MSG TEXT IS REMOTE  SP
)@@G@@@G@@@@ DO 1-RMT ,P(1,1) EQU $(QR$TLC)       . IF NOT RMT, ANCHOR TEXT HESQ
)@@G@@RE    @G@@@@QR$QC*(0) EQU       QN                . EXTERNALIZE UPDATED SR
)@@G@@QUERY CTR   @G@@@@          +         0,QR$QC(QN)-1     . OPCODE, RESPONSS
)@@G@@SE JGD COUNT COUNT@F@@@@NAW       EQU       QR$NAW(P(1,1))    . NUMBER OST
)@@G@@F ACCESS WORDS    @F@@@@AAW       EQU       (NAW>0)*QR$AAW(P(1,1)) . STASU
)@@G@@RT ADDR, IF ANY   @F@@@@          +         NAW,AAW           . ACCESS WSV
)@@G@@D FOR TEXT ACW TBL@F@@@@          QR$TXO                        . OPEN TSW
)@@G@@EXT ASSIMILATION  @#@@@@          END     @[@@@@.     @^@@@@P         PRSX
)@@G@@OC      *2  @#@@@@COMMENT** NAME    @G@@@@*         EQU       $(QR$QLC) SY
)@@G@@        . COMMENT LBL UNDER QUERY CTR     @G@@@@P(0,1)    EQU       1   SZ
)@@G@@              . FUDGE OPCODE IN RESPONSE FIELD  @E@@@@ GO QR$001        TA
)@@G@@                     . GO GENERATE TABLES @[@@@@ .    @#@@@@RESPONSE** NTB
)@@G@@AME   @F@@@@QN        EQU       QR$QC(0)          . INDEX OF CURRENT QUETC
)@@G@@RY    @G@@@@QR$QC*(QN) EQU      QR$QC(QN)+1       . COUNT RESPONSES TO TTD
)@@G@@HIS QUERY   @[@@@@ .    @F@@@@QR$001**  NAME                        . BUTE
)@@G@@ILD PACKET, JUMPTABLE   @]@@@@$(QR$TLC)   @G@@@@          QR$TXE        TF
)@@G@@              . CLOSE PRECEDING TEXT, IF ANY    @G@@@@I         EQU     TG
)@@G@@  P-1               . INDEX OF <SUB>,<EXITLIST> FIELD @G@@@@J         EQTH
)@@G@@U       3-I               . INDEX OF FIELD FOR TEXT PTR     @F@@@@RMT   TI
)@@G@@    EQU       I=2               . ON IF MSG TEXT IS REMOTE  @F@@@@JTSIZ TJ
)@@G@@    EQU       P(I)-1            . SIZE OF ALT EXIT TABLE    @E@@@@TCL   TK
)@@G@@    EQU       JTSIZ+(JTSIZ=0)   . TEXT CTR LENGTH     @E@@@@JTORG     EQTL
)@@G@@U       $(QR$TLC)         . START OF JUMPTABLE  @G@@@@ DO 1-RMT ,P(J,1) TM
)@@G@@EQU JTORG+TCL       . NON-RMT TEXT FOLLOWS JUMPTBL    @E@@@@$(QR$QLC)   TN
)@@G@@                          . START COMMAND PACKET@G@@@@          +       TO
)@@G@@  P(0,1),P(I,1)     . OPCODE/FD RESPONSE, SUBRTNE ADDR@F@@@@NAW       EQTP
)@@G@@U       QR$NAW(P(J,1))    . NUMBER OF ACCESS WORDS    @F@@@@AAW       EQTQ
)@@G@@U       (NAW>0)*QR$AAW(P(J,1)) . START ADDR, IF ANY   @F@@@@          + TR
)@@G@@        NAW,AAW           . ACCESS WD FOR TEXT ACW TBL@E@@@@          + TS
)@@G@@        JTSIZ,JTORG       . ALT RETURN TABLE ACW@F@@@@$(QR$TLC)         TT
)@@G@@                    . JUMPTABLES ON TEXT COUNTER@E@@@@K DO JTSIZ , +P(I,TU
)@@G@@K+1)                . GEN ALT EXIT JUMPTBL@G@@@@ DO JTSIZ=0 , 'FUDGE'   TV
)@@G@@              . FORCE LC BUMP SO INDEXING WORKS @F@@@@          QR$TXO  TW
)@@G@@                    . INITIALIZE TO ACCEPT TEXT @#@@@@          END     TX
)@@G@@@[@@@@.     @[@@@@.     @G@@@@          END                         . ENTY
)@@G@@D OF DEFINITION PROC, 'STARTQ'___       EQU       QR$QC(0)+1        . QUTZ
)@@G@@ERY NO FOR THIS QUERY   @F@@@@RMT       EQU       P(0)=2            . ONUA
)@@G@@*[S@@@*SDFF*@#@@@@        SAXR$     @#@@@@        STRUC$    @[@@@@ .    UB
)@@G@@@[@@@@ .    @E@@@@ . ENTER WITH 1ST QUERY ID IN A0, PACKET ADDRESS IN X1UC
)@@G@@0     @[@@@@ .    @G@@@@ . PACKET IS 3 WDS, OF WHICH 2ND MUST BE INITIALUD
)@@G@@IZED TO READ$ CONTROL,  @G@@@@ . I.E., +EOF,BUFFER. THIS ROUTINE DESTROYUE
)@@G@@S THE MINOR SET BUT PRESERVES @F@@@@ . X10.  PROCESSING RTNES (TABLE ENTUF
)@@G@@RIES) MUST NOT DESTROY X10    @[@@@@ .    @E@@@@TRPKT   EQUF    0,X10   UG
)@@G@@              . PRINT$ ACW FOR TREAD@A@@@@ . WORD 2 IS USER SUPPLIED REAUH
)@@G@@D$ CTL@^@@@@X11SAVE EQUF    2,X10   @E@@@@REPLY   EQU     TRPKT         UI
)@@G@@        . REUSE THIS WORD     @[@@@@ .    @F@@@@$(3)      LIT           UJ
)@@G@@              . FORCE LITERALS TO I-BANK  @[@@@@$(1)  @]@@@@QR$TALK*    UK
)@@G@@@^@@@@ BEGIN SUBROUTINE,NOSAVE@E@@@@   SX      X11,X11SAVE              UL
)@@G@@  . SAVE RETURN ADDRESS @F@@@@   REPEAT UNTIL A0,IS,NEG             . INUM
)@@G@@DICATING NO MORE QUERIES@H@@@@      LX,U    X11,0,A0                . SEUN
)@@G@@T UP BASE ADDR OF CURRENT QUERY     @E@@@@      IF ZERO,IN,0,X11,H1 THENUO
)@@G@@        . OPCODE IS QUERY     @F@@@@         LA,H1   A5,1,X11           UP
)@@G@@  . GET NO LINES FROM TEXT ACW@F@@@@         ANA     A5,U(1)            UQ
)@@G@@  . DON'T COUNT THE LAST ONE  @F@@@@         LA      A1,1,X11           UR
)@@G@@  . GET ADDR OF ACW TABLE     @E@@@@         LXI     A1,U(1)            US
)@@G@@  . STEP THRU BY 1 WORD @G@@@@         REPEAT JGD,A5                . LOUT
)@@G@@OP OVER ALL BUT LAST LINE     @E@@@@            LA      A0,0,*A1        UU
)@@G@@  . GET NEXT ACCESS WORD@ @@@@            ER      PRINT$    @#@@@@      UV
)@@G@@   ENDREP   @E@@@@         LA      A0,0,A1              . GET ACW OF LASUW
)@@G@@T LINE@D@@@@         . NOW ASK QUESTION BY TREAD$'ING LAST LINE   @E@@@@UX
)@@G@@         SA      A0,TRPKT             . SAVE ACW FOR PROMPT @F@@@@      UY
)@@G@@   LA,H2   A3,TRPKT+1           . GET ADDR OF INPUT BUFFER  @E@@@@      UZ
)@@G@@   LA      A0,('      ')        . GET SOME NOTHING    @F@@@@         SA VA
)@@G@@     A0,0,A3              . CLEAR 1ST WD OF INPUT     @E@@@@         SA VB
)@@G@@     A0,1,A3              . AND SECOND, TOO     @F@@@@         LA,U    AVC
)@@G@@0,TRPKT             . ADDR OF TREAD$ PACKET     @E@@@@         ER      TVD
)@@G@@READ$               . ASK THE QUESTION    @F@@@@         SA      A0,R2  VE
)@@G@@              . TEMPSAVE A0 FROM TREAD$   @D@@@@         . NOW CHECK RESVF
)@@G@@PONSE AND BRANCH ACCORDINGLY  @F@@@@         LR,H2   R1,0,X11           VG
)@@G@@  . NO OF RESPONSES LESS 1    @F@@@@         LA,H1   A0,0,A3            VH
)@@G@@  . GET 1ST 3 CHARS OF INPUT  @G@@@@         LA,U    A1,2,X11           VI
)@@G@@  . START SEARCH WITH 1ST RESPONSE  @F@@@@         AH      A1,(+3,-3)   VJ
)@@G@@        . ENTRIES ARE 3 WDS LONG    @E@@@@         SE,H1   A0,3,*A1     VK
)@@G@@        . FIND A RESPONSE     @F@@@@         NOP     0,0,*A1            VL
)@@G@@  . NOFIND => BUMP TO DEFAULT @E@@@@      ELSE                          VM
)@@G@@  . OPCODE IS COMMENT   @G@@@@         LA,U    A1,0,X11             . TRVN
)@@G@@EAT PRIMARY PACKET AS REPLY   @F@@@@      ENDIF                         VO
)@@G@@  . END OF QUERY/COMMENT TEST @E@@@@      SA      A1,REPLY              VP
)@@G@@  . SAVE REPLY POINTER  @E@@@@      . PRINT WHATEVER TEXT IS ASSOCIATED VQ
)@@G@@WITH THE REPLY    @F@@@@      LA      A2,1,A1                 . GET BASEVR
)@@G@@ OF ACW TABLE     @F@@@@      LXI     A2,U(1)                 . PRINT 1 VS
)@@G@@LINE AT A TIME    @F@@@@      REPEAT VARY,R1 FOR,1,A1,H1      . LOOP OVEVT
)@@G@@R LINES TO PRINT  @E@@@@         LA      A0,0,*A2             . GET NEXTVU
)@@G@@ ACCESS WD  @E@@@@         ER      PRINT$               . OUTPUT THE TEXVV
)@@G@@T     @F@@@@      ENDREP                          . LOOP BACK FOR NEXT LVW
)@@G@@INE   @G@@@@      LA,H2   A0,0,A1                 . GET PROCESSING SUBRTVX
)@@G@@NE ADDR     @G@@@@      IF A0,IS,NONZ THEN              . SPECIAL ACTIONVY
)@@G@@ FOR THIS REPLY   @D@@@@         LA      A1,A0                . MAKE ROOVZ
)@@G@@M     @F@@@@         LA      A0,R2                . RECOVER A0 FROM TREAWA
)@@G@@D$    @F@@@@         CALL    0,A1                 . CALL PROCESSING ROUTWB
)@@G@@INE   @G@@@@         LA      A1,REPLY             . RECOVER ADDR OF REPLWC
)@@G@@Y TABLE     @F@@@@         IF A0,GT,2,A1,H1 THEN        . REPLY INDEX OUWD
)@@G@@T OF RANGE  @F@@@@            ER      ERR$              . USER RTNE CODEWE
)@@G@@D BADLY     @#@@@@         ENDIF    @G@@@@      ENDIF                   WF
)@@G@@        . END WAS SUBROUTINE GIVEN TEST   @G@@@@      IF A0,IS,POS THEN WG
)@@G@@              . EXIT LIST SHOULD BE EXAMINED    @E@@@@         IF ZERO,IWH
)@@G@@N,2,A1,H1 THEN      . EXIT LIST IS VACUOUS@E@@@@            LNA     A0,UWI
)@@G@@(1)           . SET GLOBAL QUIT FLAG@F@@@@         ELSE                 WJ
)@@G@@        . TABLE CONTAINS EXIT LIST  @F@@@@            AU,H2   A0,2,A1   WK
)@@G@@        . ADD STARTADDR OF EXIT LIST@F@@@@            LA      A0,0,A1   WL
)@@G@@        . GET ADDR OF NEXT QUERY    @G@@@@         ENDIF                WM
)@@G@@        . END CHK FOR TABLE HAS EXIT LIST @H@@@@      ENDIF             WN
)@@G@@              . END SHOULD EXIT LIST BE USED TEST     @F@@@@   ENDREP   WO
)@@G@@                          . LOOP BACK FOR NEXT QUERY  @E@@@@   LX      XWP
)@@G@@11,X11SAVE                . RECOVER RETURN ADDR @E@@@@ ENDBEG           WQ
)@@G@@                    . RETURN TO CALLER    @[@@@@ .    @]@@@@        END WR
)@@G@@___   T     @E@@@@         SA      A0,TRPKT             . SAVE ACW FOR PWS

)@@G@@  STRUC$    @[@@@@ .    @E@@@@ . ----- DRIVER. CALLED BY MAINLINE AFTER XD
)@@G@@DETECTING @NEWS,H @[@@@@ .    @E@@@@ .       ENTER WITH A0 = ADDRESS OF XE
)@@G@@112 WORD SCRATCH AREA   @G@@@@ .       IF H1 OF X11 IS NON-ZERO, THEN LIXF
)@@G@@J CALL IS ASSUMED, ELSE LMJ   @D@@@@ .       RETURNS TO 0,X11 WITH RETURXG
)@@G@@N CODE IN A1:     @C@@@@ .               A1=0 => NORMAL END OF DIALOG   XH
)@@G@@@F@@@@ .               A1=1 => EOF ENCOUNTERED WHILE ACCEPTING INPUT    XI

)@@G@@AD$   @[@@@@ .    @G@@@@ . THIS ELEMENT IS IBANK REENTRANT, REUSABLE,  AXK
)@@G@@ND INSENSITIVE TO THE   @G@@@@ . 1/4-1/3 WORD MODE. IT HAS NO D-BANK, ANXL
)@@G@@D USES ONLY THE VOLATILE SET. @[@@@@ .    @[@@@@$(1)  @F@@@@EPSKEL    E$XM
)@@G@@PKT     15,$-$            . SKELETON EDIT$ PACKET     @E@@@@EPSIZE    EQXN
)@@G@@U       $-EPSKEL          . ITS LENGTH IN WORDS @[@@@@ .    @C@@@@ . ---XO
)@@G@@-- OUR INTERNAL PACKET AREA DEFINITION    @[@@@@ .    @[@@@@ .    @E@@@@XP
)@@G@@QRPKT   EQUF    0,X10                 . 3 WDS FOR QR$DRIVER @E@@@@X10SAVXQ
)@@G@@E EQU     QRPKT+3               . SAVE CALLER'S X10   @E@@@@HEXIT   EQU XR
)@@G@@    X10SAVE+1             . X11 SAVE FOR DRIVER @F@@@@INPBUF  EQU     HEXS

)@@G@@KT+EPSIZE           . 1ST WD USABLE BY SUBROUTINES    @[@@@@ .    @F@@@@XW
)@@G@@$(3)    LIT                           . FORCE LITERALS INTO I-BANK@[@@@@XX
)@@G@@$(1)  @]@@@@NH$START*   @^@@@@ BEGIN EXECSUB,GOODBYE  @E@@@@   SX      XXY
)@@G@@10,3,A0                   . CALLER'S X10 TO PKT @E@@@@   LX      X10,A0 XZ
)@@G@@                    . ESTABLISH OUR OWN   @E@@@@   SX      X11,HEXIT    YA
)@@G@@              . SAVE RETURN LINKAGE @F@@@@   LA,U    A3,INPBUF          YB
)@@G@@        . GET READ$ BUFFER ADDR     @D@@@@   LXI     A3,U(EOF)          YC

)@@G@@ TIME @E@@@@   LA      A1,(+1,EPSKEL)             . SKELETON PACKET     YH
)@@G@@@D@@@@   LR      R1,U(EPSIZE)               . NUMBER OF WDS @G@@@@   BT YI

)@@G@@     A0,U(NH$TBL)                . START OF DRIVER TABLES   @H@@@@   CALYO

)@@G@@CALLER WANTS IT   @E@@@@   LX      X11,HEXIT                  . GET CALLYY

)@@G@@      LIJ     X11,0,X11               . BETTER GO BACK AS WE CAME @E@@@@ZC
)@@G@@   ENDIF                              . END CALL BY LIJ TEST@]@@@@ ENDBEZD
)@@G@@G     @G@@@@/. SUBROUTINES CALLED BY TABLE INTERPRETER WHICH REALLY DO TZE
)@@G@@HE WORK     @[@@@@ .    @^@@@@P         PROC      *1  @#@@@@MASK*     NAZF
)@@G@@ME    @F@@@@K DO P-1                              ; FOR ALL ARG FIELDS..ZG
)@@G@@.     @F@@@@  , DO P(K)=1                         ; IF START/END NOT GIVZH
)@@G@@EN    @F@@@@     ,P(K,2) EQU P(K,1)               . DEFAULT TO ONE CHAR ZI
)@@G@@ONLY  @^@@@@M(1)      EQU       0D  @D@@@@K DO P-1                      ZJ
)@@G@@        ; FOR ALL FIELDS@G@@@@  ,L DO P(K,2)-P(K,1)+1               ; FOZK
)@@G@@R ALL BITS SPANNED BY FIELD   @D@@@@    ,M(1) EQU M(1)++1D*/(P(1,K)+L-1)ZL
)@@G@@ . SET THE BIT    @^@@@@          +         M(1)@#@@@@          END     ZM
)@@G@@@[@@@@$(1)  @^@@@@SPACES  '            '  @F@@@@CMASK   MASK    'A','Z' ZN
)@@G@@'0','9' '$' '-' . DEFINE MASK FOR NAMES   @F@@@@NMASK   MASK    '0','9' ZO
)@@G@@              . DEFINE MASK FOR NUMERICS  @[@@@@.     @G@@@@MONAME  EQUFZP
)@@G@@    $,,H1                 . TBL ENTRY FOR NAMES OF MONTHS   @G@@@@MODAYSZQ
)@@G@@  EQUF    $,,H2                 . TABLE ENTRY FOR NO DAYS IN MONTH@^@@@@ZR
)@@G@@        +       'JAN',31@^@@@@        +       'FEB',29@^@@@@        +   ZS
)@@G@@    'MAR',31@^@@@@        +       'APR',30@^@@@@        +       'MAY',31ZT
)@@G@@@^@@@@        +       'JUN',30@^@@@@        +       'JUL',31@^@@@@      ZU
)@@G@@  +       'AUG',31@^@@@@        +       'SEP',30@^@@@@        +       'OZV
)@@G@@CT',31@^@@@@        +       'NOV',30@^@@@@        +       'DEC',31@[@@@@ZW
)@@G@@ .    @D@@@@ . ----- SCRATCH FIELDS WHICH USE PACKET WORDS ...    @[@@@@ZX
)@@G@@ .    @G@@@@MAXDAYS EQUF    SCRATCH,,S1           . TEMPSAVE DAYS IN SELZY
)@@G@@ECTED MONTH @F@@@@OPTCHAR EQUF    SCRATCH,,S2           . TEMPSAVE OPTIOZZ
)@@G@@NS CHARACTER@G@@@@OPTCOL  EQUF    SCRATCH,,S3           . TEMPSAVE CURREAA
)@@G@@NT OPTIONS COLUMN @G@@@@SPECHAR EQUF    SCRATCH,,S4           . TEMPSAVEAB
)@@G@@ LEADING CHAR OF SPEC   @H@@@@SPECOL  EQUF    SCRATCH,,Q4           . TEAC
)@@G@@MPSAVE COLUMN FOR SPECS (Q4=T3)     @G@@@@BKUPCHR EQUF    SCRATCH+1,,S1 AD
)@@G@@        . TEMPSAVE TO BACK UP OVER MONTH  @G@@@@BKUPCOL EQUF    SCRATCH+AE
)@@G@@1,,S2         . TEMPSAVE TO BACK UP OVER MONTH  @F@@@@SPECSIZ EQUF    SCAF
)@@G@@RATCH+1,,S3         . SIZE (NO OF CHARS) IN SPEC@G@@@@ITRAIL  EQUF    SCAG
)@@G@@RATCH+1,,S4         . TEMPSAVE TRAILING SPEC CHAR     @F@@@@KOPTFLG EQUFAH
)@@G@@    SCRATCH+1,,S5         . FLAG SET FOR 'K' OPTION   @F@@@@NOPTFLG EQUFAI
)@@G@@    SCRATCH+1,,S6         . FLAG SET FOR 'N' OPTION   @F@@@@MAXWID  EQUFAJ
)@@G@@    SCRATCH+2,,S1         . TEMPSAVE MAX FIELD WIDTH  @G@@@@XRSTAK  EQU AK
)@@G@@    SCRATCH+3             . 1ST AVAIL LOC FOR X11 SAVES     @[@@@@ .    AL
)@@G@@@F@@@@ . SETUP FOR AUTO ASSIGNMENT OF SAVE WORDS FOR X11 IN SCRATCH AREAAM
)@@G@@@[@@@@ .    @]@@@@F       FUNC@G@@@@NXTEMP* NAME                        AN
)@@G@@  . BUMP OFFSET TO NEXT AVAIL LOCN  @ @@@@XRTMP**(0) EQU  XRTMP(0)+1    AO
)@@G@@@ @@@@        END     +XRTMP(0)     @[@@@@.     @F@@@@XRTMP(0) EQU    XRAP
)@@G@@STAK-QRPKT-1        . OFFSET -1 TO 1ST LOCN     @[@@@@ .    @[@@@@.     AQ
)@@G@@@A@@@@ . ----- STANDARD CONTROL VALUES    @[@@@@ .    @F@@@@ICOPTS  EQU AR
)@@G@@    U(5)                  . INITIAL COLUMN FOR OPTIONS@F@@@@ICSPECS EQU AS
)@@G@@    U(12)                 . INITIAL COLUMN FOR SPECS  @[@@@@ .    @F@@@@AT
)@@G@@ . STANDARD EXIT CODES FOR SUBROUTINES WHICH PROCESS SPEC FIELDS  @[@@@@AU
)@@G@@ .    @E@@@@ILCHAR  EQU     U(0)                  . EXIT CODE FOR ILCHARAV
)@@G@@@G@@@@NULLANS EQU     U(1)                  . EXIT CODE FOR NULL REPLY (AW
)@@G@@CR)   @G@@@@VALID   EQU     U(2)                  . NORMAL EXIT, FIELD IAX
)@@G@@S EDITED    @G@@@@CMDFULL EQU     U(3)                  . SPEC WON'T FITAY
)@@G@@ ON CARD IMAGE    @F@@@@RANGERR EQU     U(4)                  . RANGE ERAZ
)@@G@@ROR, NUMERIC SPEC @[@@@@ .    @[@@@@$(1)  @[@@@@ .    @E@@@@ . INITIALIZBA
)@@G@@E THE @NEWS IMAGE AND EDIT$ AND OTHER FLAGS     @[@@@@ .    @]@@@@NH$SETBB
)@@G@@UP*   @F@@@@ BEGIN SUBROUTINE,NOSAVE STACK,X11,POINTER,X10 OFFSET,NXTEMPBC
)@@G@@(0)   @D@@@@   E$CLEAR                            . CLEAR IMAGE   @E@@@@BD
)@@G@@   E$COPY  5,('@NEWS ')               . INITIALIZE COMMAND  @F@@@@   LA BE
)@@G@@     A0,ICOPTS                  . GET START COL FOR OPTIONS @E@@@@   LA BF
)@@G@@     A1,ICSPECS                 . START COL FOR SPECS @^@@@@   LA      ABG
)@@G@@2,U(' ')    @F@@@@   SA      A0,OPTCOL                  . SAVE 'NEXT' OPBH
)@@G@@TIONS COLUMN@E@@@@   SA      A1,SPECOL                  . SAVE NEXT SPECBI
)@@G@@ COL  @G@@@@   SA      A2,SPECHAR                 . SAVE LEADING CHAR FOBJ
)@@G@@R NEXT SPEC @E@@@@   LA      A0,U(0)                    . TAKE NORMAL EXBK
)@@G@@IT    @F@@@@   SZ      KOPTFLG                    . CLEAR KEYWORD LIST FBL
)@@G@@LAG   @G@@@@   SZ      NOPTFLG                    . CLEAR SEQUENCE NO LIBM
)@@G@@ST FLAG     @]@@@@ ENDBEG     @[@@@@ .    @C@@@@ . ADD AN OPTION LETTER BN
)@@G@@TO THE @NEWS COMMAND    @[@@@@ .    @^@@@@NH$AOPT* LA,U   A0,'A'  @^@@@@BO
)@@G@@        J       OPTIONS @^@@@@NH$GOPT* LA,U   A0,'G'  @^@@@@        J   BP
)@@G@@    OPTIONS @^@@@@NH$KOPT* LA,U   A0,'K'  @G@@@@        SA      A0,KOPTFBQ
)@@G@@LG            . TURN KEYWORD LISTING FLAG ON    @^@@@@        J       OPBR
)@@G@@TIONS @^@@@@NH$LOPT* LA,U   A0,'L'  @^@@@@        J       OPTIONS @^@@@@BS
)@@G@@NH$NOPT* LA,U   A0,'N'  @G@@@@        SA      A0,NOPTFLG            . TUBT
)@@G@@RN SEQUENCE LISTING FLAG ON   @^@@@@        J       OPTIONS @^@@@@NH$ROPBU
)@@G@@T* LA,U   A0,'R'  @^@@@@        J       OPTIONS @^@@@@NH$OOPT* LA,U   A0BV
)@@G@@,'O'  @^@@@@        J       OPTIONS @^@@@@NH$MOPT* LA,U   A0,'M'  @[@@@@BW
)@@G@@ .    @]@@@@OPTIONS     @F@@@@ BEGIN SUBROUTINE,NOSAVE STACK,X11,POINTERBX
)@@G@@,X10 OFFSET,NXTEMP(0)   @F@@@@   SA      A0,OPTCHAR                 . TEBY
)@@G@@MPSAVE OPTIONS CHAR     @F@@@@   LA      A0,OPTCOL                  . GEBZ
)@@G@@T COL FOR NEXT OPTION   @D@@@@   E$COL                              . POCA
)@@G@@SITION TO IT@E@@@@   LA      A0,OPTCOL                  . RECOVER OPTIONCB
)@@G@@S COL @E@@@@   IF A0,EQ,ICOPTS   THEN             . THIS IS FIRST OPTIONCC
)@@G@@@F@@@@      E$CHAR  ','                     . PLUG IN LEADING COMMA     CD
)@@G@@@G@@@@   ENDIF                              . END LEADING COMMA NEEDED TCE
)@@G@@EST   @F@@@@   LA      A0,OPTCHAR                 . RETRIEVE OPTIONS CHACF
)@@G@@RACTER@D@@@@   E$CHAR                             . PLUG IT IN    @F@@@@CG
)@@G@@   E$COLN                             . FIND OUT WHERE WE ARE     @D@@@@CH
)@@G@@   SA      A0,OPTCOL                  . AND REMEMBER  @D@@@@   LA      ACI
)@@G@@0,U(0)                    . NORMAL EXIT   @]@@@@ ENDBEG     @[@@@@ .    CJ
)@@G@@@E@@@@NH$KOTST* LA      A0,KOPTFLG            . GET K-OPTION FLAG @D@@@@CK
)@@G@@        J       OPTEST                . GO CHECK IT   @E@@@@NH$NOTST* LACL
)@@G@@      A0,NOPTFLG            . GET N-OPTION FLAG @[@@@@ .    @[@@@@OPTESTCM
)@@G@@@^@@@@ BEGIN SUBROUTINE,NOSAVE@D@@@@   IF A0,IS,NONZ THEN               CN
)@@G@@  . OPTION IS SET @D@@@@      LA      A0,U(1)                 . TAKE SETCO
)@@G@@ EXIT @]@@@@   ENDIF    @]@@@@ ENDBEG     @E@@@@/. ----- UTILITY SUBROUTCP
)@@G@@INES CALLED BY SPEC FIELD HANDLERS  @[@@@@ .    @[@@@@$(1)  @[@@@@ .    CQ
)@@G@@@E@@@@ . ----- COPY FIXED NO CHARS FROM INPUT TO NEXT SPEC FIELD  @F@@@@CR
)@@G@@ .       ENTRY CONDNS: GLOBAL 'SPECSIZ' SET TO NO OF CHARS TO EDIT@G@@@@CS
)@@G@@ .                     A1 = MAX WIDTH FOR FIELD (TO CHECK FULL CARD)    CT
)@@G@@@[@@@@ .    @[@@@@ .    @G@@@@SCOPYSL LA      A0,U('/')             . SPCU
)@@G@@ECIAL CASE => TRAILING SLASH  @^@@@@        J       SPCOPY  @F@@@@SPECOPCV
)@@G@@Y LA      A0,U(',')             . NORMAL CASE TRAILING COMMA@[@@@@ .    CW
)@@G@@@[@@@@SPCOPY@F@@@@ BEGIN SUBROUTINE,NOSAVE STACK,X11,POINTER,X10 OFFSET,CX
)@@G@@NXTEMP(0)   @H@@@@   SA      A1,MAXWID                  . SAVE MAX WIDTHCY
)@@G@@ OF THIS TYPE FIELD     @G@@@@   SA      A0,ITRAIL                  . SACZ
)@@G@@VE TRAILING CHAR FOR THIS SPEC@G@@@@   LA      A0,SPECOL                DA
)@@G@@  . GET COL WHERE THIS SPEC STARTS  @D@@@@   E$COL                      DB
)@@G@@        . POSITION THERE@G@@@@   LA      A0,SPECHAR                 . GEDC
)@@G@@T LEADING CHAR FOR THIS SPEC  @D@@@@   E$CHAR                           DD
)@@G@@  . PLUG IT IN    @G@@@@   LA      A5,ITRAIL                  . RECOVER DE
)@@G@@CHAR FOR NEXT FIELD     @F@@@@   LA      A1,SPECSIZ                 . GEDF
)@@G@@T NO OF CHARS TO COPY   @F@@@@   LA,U    A0,INPBUF                  . SODG
)@@G@@URCE IS INPUT BUFFER    @G@@@@   SA      A5,SPECHAR                 . SEDH
)@@G@@T STARTCHAR FOR NEXT SPEC     @F@@@@   E$COPY                           DI
)@@G@@  . COPY SPECIFIED NO OF CHARS@G@@@@   E$COLN                           DJ
)@@G@@  . FIND OUT WHICH COLUMN WE'RE AT  @F@@@@   SA      A0,SPECOL          DK
)@@G@@        . SAVE CURRENT CARD COLUMN  @H@@@@   AU      A0,MAXWID          DL
)@@G@@        . PLUS MAX WIDTH OF CURRENT TYPE FIELD  @E@@@@   LA      A0,VALIDM
)@@G@@D                   . SET NORMAL EXIT FLAG@F@@@@   IF A1,GE,U(78) THEN  DN
)@@G@@              . NO MORE FIELDS WILL FIT   @E@@@@      LA      A0,CMDFULLDO
)@@G@@              . GET BUFFER FULL CODE@]@@@@   ENDIF    @C@@@@ ENDBEG     DP
)@@G@@                          . RETURN  @[@@@@ .    @B@@@@ . ------ CHECK INDQ
)@@G@@PUT FOR AN ALFA NAME    @D@@@@ .        EXITS: A0=0 => ILCHAR OR LEADINGDR
)@@G@@ SPACES     @F@@@@ .               A0=1 => USER REPLY BLANK (I.E. CARRIADS
)@@G@@GE RETURN)  @D@@@@ .               A0=2 => OK. NO OF CHARS LEFT IN A1   DT
)@@G@@@[@@@@ .    @[@@@@ .    @[@@@@ANCHEK@F@@@@ BEGIN SUBROUTINE,NOSAVE STACKDU
)@@G@@,X11,POINTER,X10 OFFSET,NXTEMP(0)   @F@@@@   DL      A4,INPBUF          DV
)@@G@@        . GET 1ST 2 WDS OF INPUT    @E@@@@   LA      A0,NULLANS         DW
)@@G@@        . ASSUME ITS BLANKS   @E@@@@   IF A4,DNE,SPACES THEN            DX
)@@G@@  . USER TYPED SOMETHING@E@@@@      LA      A0,VALID                . ASDY
)@@G@@SUME ITS VALID    @E@@@@      REPEAT VARY,R1 FOR,U(12)        . LOOP OVEDZ
)@@G@@R MAX CHARS @F@@@@         LA      A3,U(0)              . CLEAR CHAR EXAEA
)@@G@@MINE REG    @F@@@@         LDSL    A3,6                 . NEXT CHAR FROMEB
)@@G@@ A4 TO A3   @E@@@@         DL      A1,CMASK             . GET CHARACTER EC
)@@G@@MASK  @F@@@@         DSL     A1,0,A3              . ALIGN BIT FOR THIS CED
)@@G@@HAR   @F@@@@      ESCAPE WHEN A2,IS,EVEN          . CHAR IS NOT IN NAME EE
)@@G@@SET   @E@@@@         IF A3,NE,U(' ') THEN         . NON SPACE => ILCHAR EF
)@@G@@@E@@@@            LA      A0,ILCHAR         . SET ILCHAR FLAG     @#@@@@EG
)@@G@@         ENDIF    @E@@@@      OTHERWISE                       . CHAR IS EH
)@@G@@IN NAME SET @E@@@@         SSL     A4,6                 . REALIGN LEFT HEI
)@@G@@ALF   @F@@@@         LDSL    A4,6                 . AND CATENATE RIGHT BEJ
)@@G@@ACK ON@F@@@@      ENDREP                          . LOOP BACK FOR NEXT CEK
)@@G@@HAR   @F@@@@      LA      A1,U(11)                . GET BASE FOR CHAR COEL
)@@G@@UNT   @F@@@@      ANA     A1,R1                   . COMPUTE NO OF LEGAL EM
)@@G@@CHARS @D@@@@      IF A1,IS,ZERO THEN              . NO VALID CHARS@D@@@@EN
)@@G@@         LA      A0,ILCHAR            . SET ERROR FLAG@F@@@@      ENDIF EO
)@@G@@                          . END ANY CHARS SEEN TEST   @F@@@@      IF A0,EP
)@@G@@EQ,VALID THEN             . PUT RESULT IN COMMAND     @E@@@@         SA EQ
)@@G@@     A1,SPECSIZ           . SET UP NO OF CHARS  @F@@@@         LA      AER
)@@G@@1,U(12)             . SET UP MAX FIELD WIDTH    @F@@@@         CALL    SES
)@@G@@PECOPY              . COPY THEN FROM THE BUFFER @F@@@@      ENDIF       ET
)@@G@@                    . END OF SHOULD WE COPY TEST@G@@@@   ENDIF          EU
)@@G@@                    . END WAS REPLY ALL SPACES TEST   @C@@@@ ENDBEG     EV
)@@G@@                          . RETURN  @[@@@@ .    @[@@@@ .    @D@@@@ . ---EW
)@@G@@-- CHECK NUMERIC SPECIFICATIONS AND EDIT THEM IN@C@@@@ .       ENTER WITEX
)@@G@@H A0 = MAXVAL FOR RANGE CHECK @[@@@@ .    @[@@@@NUMCHK@F@@@@ BEGIN SUBROEY
)@@G@@UTINE,NOSAVE STACK,X11,POINTER,X10 OFFSET,NXTEMP(0)   @G@@@@   SA      AEZ
)@@G@@0,R3                      . TEMP SAVE MAX ALLOWED VALUE     @D@@@@   LA FA
)@@G@@     A2,INPBUF                  . GET INPUT DATA@F@@@@   LA      A3,SPACFB
)@@G@@ES                  . GUARANTEE LOOP TERMINATION@G@@@@   LA      A0,NULLFC
)@@G@@ANS                 . ASSUME USER GAVE NULL REPLY     @E@@@@   IF A2,NE,FD
)@@G@@A3 THEN                   . USER TYPED SOMETHING@F@@@@      LX      X11,FE
)@@G@@U(0)                . INITIALIZE CHAR COUNTER   @F@@@@      LA      A1,UFF
)@@G@@(0)                 . CLEAR ACCUMULATED SUM     @F@@@@      REPEAT      FG
)@@G@@                    . LOOP OVER CHARS OF INPUT  @F@@@@         LXM     AFH
)@@G@@3,U(0)              . CLEAR LOWER FOR INDEXING  @F@@@@         LDSC    AFI
)@@G@@2,6                 . NEXT CHAR TO A3 LOWER     @D@@@@         DL      AFJ
)@@G@@4,NMASK             . GET CTL BITS  @F@@@@         DSL     A4,0,A3      FK
)@@G@@        . ALIGN BIT FOR THIS CHAR   @E@@@@      ESCAPE WHEN A5,IS,EVEN  FL
)@@G@@        . CHAR IS NON-DIGIT   @D@@@@      OTHERWISE                     FM
)@@G@@  . PROCESS DIGIT @F@@@@         AND     A3,U(017)            . ISOLATE FN
)@@G@@ITS BINARY VALUE  @E@@@@         MSI     A1,U(10)             . BUMP RUNFO
)@@G@@NING SUM    @E@@@@         AX      X11,U(1)             . COUNT THIS DIGFP
)@@G@@IT    @E@@@@         AA      A1,A4                . ADD BIN VALUE TO SUMFQ
)@@G@@@F@@@@      ENDREP                          . LOOP BACK FOR NEXT DIGIT  FR
)@@G@@@B@@@@      . AT EXIT, A3 LOWER = 1ST NON-DIGIT @F@@@@      LXI     A3,UFS
)@@G@@(0)                 . CLEAR UPPER FOR COMPARE   @E@@@@      LA      A0,IFT
)@@G@@LCHAR               . ASSUME FORMAT ERROR @F@@@@      IF NONZ,IN,X11 ANDFU
)@@G@@ A3,EQ,U(' ') THEN . GOT DIGITS,..., SPACE@F@@@@         LA      A0,RANGFV
)@@G@@ERR           . ASSUME VALUE OUT OF RANGE @E@@@@         IF A1,GE,U(1) AFW
)@@G@@ND A1,LE,R3 THEN . VALUE IS IN RANGE@E@@@@            SX      X11,SPECSIFX
)@@G@@Z       . TEMPSAVE NO OF CHARS@G@@@@            LA      A1,U(5)         FY
)@@G@@  . GET MAX WIDTH OF NUMERIC FIELDS @F@@@@            CALL    SPECOPY   FZ
)@@G@@        . COPY THE SPECIFICATION    @E@@@@         ENDIF                GA
)@@G@@        . END OF RANGE CHECK  @E@@@@      ENDIF                         GB
)@@G@@  . END OF ILCHAR CHECK @E@@@@   ENDIF                              . ENGC
)@@G@@D OF SPACES CHECK @]@@@@ ENDBEG     @B@@@@/. ROUTINES TO PROCESS SPEC FIGD
)@@G@@ELD INPUTS  @[@@@@ .    @G@@@@ . SCAN INPUT FOR GROUP NAME, VERIFY IT, AGE
)@@G@@ND ADD TO THE @NEWS IMAGE     @[@@@@ .    @]@@@@NH$GRSCN*   @F@@@@ BEGINGF
)@@G@@ SUBROUTINE,NOSAVE STACK,X11,POINTER,X10 OFFSET,NXTEMP(0)   @G@@@@   CALGG
)@@G@@L    ANCHEK                     . IF NAME VALID, PLUG INTO BUFFER @D@@@@GH
)@@G@@   IF A0,EQ,VALID THEN                . WE DID IT     @E@@@@      CALL  GI
)@@G@@  NH$GOPT                 . PUT ON THE OPTION   @F@@@@      LA      A0,VGJ
)@@G@@ALID                . RESTORE THE EXIT FLAG     @]@@@@   ENDIF    @]@@@@GK
)@@G@@ ENDBEG     @[@@@@ .    @D@@@@ . SCAN INPUT FOR SEQUENCE NUMBER, APPEND GL
)@@G@@TO IMAGE    @[@@@@ .    @]@@@@NH$SQSCN*   @F@@@@ BEGIN SUBROUTINE,NOSAVEGM
)@@G@@ STACK,X11,POINTER,X10 OFFSET,NXTEMP(0)   @F@@@@   LA      A0,U(99999)  GN
)@@G@@              . RANGE ESSENTIALLY INFINITE@G@@@@   CALL    NUMCHK       GO
)@@G@@              . CHECK AND EDIT NUMERIC FIELD    @]@@@@ ENDBEG     @[@@@@GP
)@@G@@ .    @B@@@@ . SCAN INPUT FOR NUMBER OF DAYS SINCE... @[@@@@ .    @]@@@@GQ
)@@G@@NH$NDSCN*   @F@@@@ BEGIN SUBROUTINE,NOSAVE STACK,X11,POINTER,X10 OFFSET,GR
)@@G@@NXTEMP(0)   @D@@@@   LA      A0,U(30)                   . MAX IS 30 DAYSGS
)@@G@@@#@@@@   CALL    NUMCHK @]@@@@ ENDBEG     @[@@@@ .    @B@@@@ . SCAN FOR GT
)@@G@@KEYWORD AND EDIT ONTO IMAGE   @[@@@@ .    @H@@@@NH$KWSCN* EQU     ANCHEKGU
)@@G@@                . KEYWORDS ARE STANDARD A/N FIELDS    @E@@@@/. PROCESS SGV
)@@G@@PECS FOR MONTH/DAY SPECIFICATION OF CUTOFF DATE @[@@@@ .    @F@@@@ . SCAGW
)@@G@@N INPUT FOR NAME OF MONTH, VERIFY IT, ADD TO THE @NEWS IMAGE@[@@@@ .    GX
)@@G@@@[@@@@ .    @]@@@@NH$MOSCN*   @F@@@@ BEGIN SUBROUTINE,NOSAVE STACK,X11,PGY
)@@G@@OINTER,X10 OFFSET,NXTEMP(0)   @E@@@@   LA      A5,INPBUF                GZ
)@@G@@  . GET 1ST WD OF INPUT @F@@@@   LA      A0,NULLANS                 . ASHA
)@@G@@SUME USER TYPED RETURN  @E@@@@   IF A5,NE,SPACES THEN               . HEHB
)@@G@@ GAVE US SOMETHING@E@@@@      LA      A0,ILCHAR               . ASSUME IHC
)@@G@@TS AN ERROR @G@@@@      SSL     A5,18                   . ALIGN 1ST 3 CHHD
)@@G@@ARS OF RESPONSE   @E@@@@      IF LOOKFOR A5,EQ,MONAME ;       . FIND MONHE
)@@G@@TH IN TABLE @D@@@@         VARY,A2,OFFSET FROM,U(0) BY,U(1) FOR,U(12)   HF
)@@G@@@G@@@@         LA      A3,SPECOL            . GET CURRENT OUTPUT IMAGE CHG
)@@G@@OL    @E@@@@         LA      A4,SPECHAR           . AND LEADING CHAR    HH
)@@G@@@F@@@@         LA      A5,MODAYS,A2         . GET NO OF DAYS TO EXPECT  HI
)@@G@@@E@@@@         SA      A3,BKUPCOL           . SET COLUMN BACKUP   @F@@@@HJ
)@@G@@         LA      A3,U(3)              . MONTHS ALWAYS 3 CHARS LONG@E@@@@HK
)@@G@@         SA      A4,BKUPCHR           . AND BACKUP CHAR     @F@@@@      HL
)@@G@@   SA      A5,MAXDAYS           . TEMPSAVE FOR DAY CHECK    @F@@@@      HM
)@@G@@   SA      A3,SPECSIZ           . SET NO OF CHARS IN SPEC   @G@@@@      HN
)@@G@@   CALL    SCOPYSL              . COPY MONTH WITH TRAILING SLASH  @F@@@@HO
)@@G@@      ENDIF                           . END WAS MONTH LEGAL TEST  @G@@@@HP
)@@G@@   ENDIF                              . END TEST FOR DID USER GIVE UP   HQ
)@@G@@@]@@@@ ENDBEG     @[@@@@ .    @F@@@@ . SCAN INPUT FOR DAY IN MONTH, VERIHR
)@@G@@FY, AND ADD TO @NEWS IMAGE    @[@@@@ .    @]@@@@NH$DASCN*   @F@@@@ BEGINHS
)@@G@@ SUBROUTINE,NOSAVE STACK,X11,POINTER,X10 OFFSET,NXTEMP(0)   @G@@@@   LA HT
)@@G@@     A0,MAXDAYS                 . GET MAX DAYS ALLOWED IN MONTH   @D@@@@HU
)@@G@@   CALL    NUMCHK                     . CHECK AND EDIT@]@@@@ ENDBEG     HV
)@@G@@@[@@@@ .    @F@@@@ . ----- ABORT MONTH/DAY. BACK COLUMNS UP TO WHERE MONHW
)@@G@@TH STARTED  @[@@@@ .    @]@@@@NH$DBKUP*   @^@@@@ BEGIN SUBROUTINE,NOSAVEHX
)@@G@@@^@@@@   LA      A3,BKUPCOL   @^@@@@   LA      A4,BKUPCHR   @E@@@@   LA HY
)@@G@@     A0,U(0)                    . NORMAL EXIT FLAG    @F@@@@   SA      AHZ
)@@G@@3,SPECOL                  . RESET COL TO START OF SPEC@F@@@@   SA      AIA
)@@G@@4,SPECHAR                 . AND CHAR TO LEADING VALUE @]@@@@ ENDBEG     IB
)@@G@@@[@@@@ .    @[@@@@ .    @ @@@@/. CLEANUP AND EXIT ROUTINES  @[@@@@ .    IC
)@@G@@@[@@@@ .    @]@@@@NH$PCMD*    @F@@@@ BEGIN SUBROUTINE,NOSAVE STACK,X11,PID
)@@G@@OINTER,X10 OFFSET,NXTEMP(0)   @F@@@@   LA      A0,SPECOL                IE
)@@G@@  . GET NEXT COL IN SPEC FIELD@D@@@@   E$COL                            IF
)@@G@@  . POSITION TO IT@E@@@@   E$CHAR  077                        . PLUG IN IG
)@@G@@A PRINT STOP@D@@@@   LA      A0,SPECOL                  . RECOVER IT    IH
)@@G@@@E@@@@   AA      A0,U(6)                    . ROUND TO WORD BNDRY @E@@@@II
)@@G@@   DSL     A0,36                      . SETUP FOR DIVIDE    @E@@@@   DI IJ
)@@G@@     A0,U(6)                    . CONVERT TO WORD CNT @G@@@@   LXI,U   AIK
)@@G@@0,0100,A0                 . WDCT TO H1 WITH SKIPCNT ADDED   @F@@@@   LXMIL
)@@G@@,U   A0,CMDBUF                  . SET START ADDR OF BUFF    @D@@@@   ER IM
)@@G@@     PRINT$                     . DISPLAY IT    @E@@@@   LA      A0,U(0)IN
)@@G@@                    . SET NORMAL EXIT FLAG@]@@@@ ENDBEG     @[@@@@ .    IO
)@@G@@@]@@@@NH$DONE*    @^@@@@ BEGIN SUBROUTINE,NOSAVE@H@@@@   LNA     A0,U(1)IP
)@@G@@                    . TERMINATE TABLE INTREPRETATION MODE   @]@@@@ ENDBEIQ
)@@G@@G     @[@@@@ .    @#@@@@          END     ___ANDUTINE,NOSAVE@H@@@@   LNAIR
)@@G@@     A0,U(1)                    . TERMINATE TABLE INTREPRETATION MODE   IS
)@@G@@@]@@@@ ENDBEG     @[@@@@ .    @#@@@@          EN)@@[U@@@K@@@&;0@@TC8'@@ IT
